Location: Very, very remote, far away from Yangshuo County. Ten-mile Gallery, Yulong River rafting, and some Internet celebrity check-in spots, West Street round trip takes 45-60 minutes. Rafting: Don't believe the rafting provided by the hotel. It's a river at the door of the hotel. The water is very turbid and there is garbage at the dock. It takes 50 minutes to go back and forth, and there is almost no scenery. It is so different from Yulong River.
Clothing: Dissuade sisters. The so-called travel photography and clothing provided, my gosh, they are ugly and dirty, so I decisively gave up.
Hygiene: The hygiene of the restaurant is worrying. There is a smell of stinky bamboo shoots inside, and there are female peacocks walking around freely outside. The table and the feet are full of their food residues. It is horrible.

Small bridges, flowing water, pavilions, pavilions and pavilions complement each other, and the vegetation is rich and lush. Looking at the lush greenery, it is indeed a secret place to hide from the world. There are peacocks walking freely in the park, colorful koi and ducks in the pond, and you can also feed alpacas and little fragrant pigs regularly.
The location of Banyan Tree is relatively remote, which is more suitable for vacation, recuperation and relaxation. You can only drive or charter a car to visit the surrounding attractions. The hotel provides a shuttle bus to West Street.
The hotel room facilities fully reflect its sense of age, which does not match the star rating of the hotel. The facilities are relatively old, the bathroom has a peculiar smell, the mattress is very uncomfortable, and the sound is loud when you move it a little. The power socket in the room is loose and unreal, which affects the use.
The hotel's breakfast tastes very good, divided into Chinese and Western styles. There are also a lot of varieties. My favorite is small rice in bamboo tube and rice noodles in soup. The environment is a small villa, and there are also suites. This time we stayed in a suite. The space design and layout are also very comfortable. There is a small balcony outside the suite. The scenery is very good and you can see the mountains, so this room is also called the mountains. impression. There are also battery cars to pick up and drop off, which is very convenient. I chose 4 o'clock in the afternoon, the sun was still a little big, so I suggest that the ladies can choose around 5 o'clock, or 9 or 10 in the morning, because the morning sun in the lobby can just reflect on the face, and in the afternoon it will be Backlight, also see their options. The picture below was taken by my family's mobile phone, not by the photographer.
The first time I stayed at Banyan Tree in Phuket was many years ago. There was no epidemic at that time. This time it was in Yangshuo.
